<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:commercie.html>commercie</a> (32735)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">commerce</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">commercium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">commerce, trade</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">com-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">merx</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">good, wares, merchandise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">merchant</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mercenary</i>.
</p>

***commissie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:commissie.html>commissie</a> (3716)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">commission</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">commissio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sending together; commission</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from prefix <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">com-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">with</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, + noun of action <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">missio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sending</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> passive participle <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">missus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mittō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to send</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, + noun of action <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-io</i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:commotie.html>commotie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">commocion</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">commōtiō</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">commōtus</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> passive participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">commoveō</i>.

***communie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:communie.html>communie</a> (12478)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:communie.html>communie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">communion</i>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Roman Catholicism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> communion</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***communisme.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:communisme.html>communisme</a> (12105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:communisme.html>communisme</a></i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kommunismus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:communisme.html>communisme</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:communisme.html>communismen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:communisme.html>communismetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>communism <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">collectivist socialism, ideology</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:communisme.html>communisme</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> Sovjetblok <a href = vnd.unilang:verloor.html>verloor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koude.html>Koude</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorlog.html>Oorlog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:westers.html>Westers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kapitalisme.html>kapitalisme</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:val.html>val</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muur.html>Muur</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The Soviet block's <b>Communism</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> the Cold War against Western capitalism when the Wall <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> down.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>communism <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">classless and stateless international socialist order</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Marx <a href = vnd.unilang:voorspelde.html>voorspelde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:communisme.html>communisme</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> eindstadium <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontwikkeling.html>ontwikkeling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wereldorde.html>wereldorde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Marx predicted that <b>communism</b> would be the final stage of the development of the world order.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> any collectivism
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:communisme.html>communisme</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Babeuf <a href = vnd.unilang:dateert.html>dateert</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:directoire.html>Directoire</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:generaties.html>generaties</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:karl.html>Karl</a> Marx' Manifest.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Babeuf's <b>communism</b> dates from the <a href = vnd.unilang:directoire.html>Directoire</a>, generations before <a href = vnd.unilang:karl.html>Karl</a> Marx's Manifesto.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">collectivisme</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:compositie.html>compositie</a> (25411)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">composicie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">composition</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">composicion</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">compositiō</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:componeren.html>componere</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to put together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The modern spelling <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">composition</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:compositie.html>compositie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:composities.html>composities</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:compositie.html>compositietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The composition (general) makeup of something, notably in <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> of components such as ingredients; especially a (metallic) alloy</li>
<li>A musical composition, piece written by a composer</li>
<li>An artistic composition, arrangement as of figures in a scene, colors on a canvas etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">treaty</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">contract</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">settlement</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">general makeup</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:samenstelling.html>samenstelling</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">musical piece</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">muziekstuk</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">component</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:componeren.html>componeren</a></span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:concentratiekamp.html>concentratiekamp</a> (15445)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:concentratie.html>concentratie</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamp.html>kamp</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">concentration camp</i>. Attested since the late nineteenth century (see citation page).
</p>

***concertina.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a> (94485)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">concertinas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A musical instrument, like the various accordions, that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a member of the free-reed family of musical instruments, typically having <a href = vnd.unilang:buttons.html>buttons</a> on both <a href = vnd.unilang:ends.html>ends</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_C._Lincoln" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Joseph C. Lincoln">Joseph C. Lincoln</a>,  chapter 8, in  <cite><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL5535161W"><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. Pratt's Patients</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">That <b><a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a wonder in its way. The handles that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> on it first <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> wore out long ago, and he'd made new <a href = vnd.unilang:ones.html>ones</a> of braided rope yarn. And the <a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> patched in more <a href = vnd.unilang:places.html>places</a> than a cranberry <a href = vnd.unilang:picker.html>picker</a>'s <a href = vnd.unilang:overalls.html>overalls</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Something resembling a <a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a>, such as a folded book, a <a href = vnd.unilang:bus.html>bus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> or a set of picture <a href = vnd.unilang:frames.html>frames</a> that are folded together.</li>
<li>Coiled barbed wire for use as an obstacle.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup></li>
<li>A type of booklet label, consisting of up to 32 pages of booklet as an insert.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">concertinas</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">concertinaing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">concertinaed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become compressed into a shape reminiscent of a <a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a>
<dl><dd><i>The car <b>concertinaed</b> into the wall.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2012</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:amy.html>Amy</a> Schoeman, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Skeleton_Coast" class="extiw" title="w:Skeleton Coast">Skeleton Coast</a></i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.ru/books?id=W75aoZLDG9YCamp;lpg=RA1-PR2amp;dq=concertinaedamp;pg=RA1-PR2v=onepageamp;q=concertinaedamp;f=false">page ii</a>
<dl><dd>Millions of years ago the <a href = vnd.unilang:mica.html>mica</a> schists surrounding the old Brandberg West Mine became folded and <b>concertinaed</b> by enormous horizontal pressures.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>to be drawn <a href = vnd.unilang:closer.html>closer</a> and farther apart repeatedly, or up and down, as if situated on a working <a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a>'s folds
<ul><li><b>2007</b>, David W Cameron, <i>25 April 1915: The Day the Anzac Legend <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>Was</a> Born</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.ru/books?id=XyxIQIg0TPcCamp;lpg=PA36amp;dq=concertinaedamp;pg=PA36v=onepageamp;q=concertinaedamp;f=false">page 36</a>
<dl><dd>This resulted in some fragmentation of the line as the <a href = vnd.unilang:boats.html>boats</a> in some <a href = vnd.unilang:cases.html>cases</a> closed to just 50 metres as they <b>concertinaed</b> in and out of sight of each other.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:muziekinstrument.html>muziekinstrument</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> trekzak gelijkende <a href = vnd.unilang:kleine.html>kleine</a>, zeshoekige <a href = vnd.unilang:accordeon.html>accordeon</a></li></ol>
<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Verwante_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:verwante.html>Verwante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li>bandoneon</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> concerto (16685)</h1><br></body>
